<Text>After years of driving past I finally tried this place. It is prominently located on the end of a strip mall and see it every time I drive by.

So we go in and it is very spacious and well lit, there are no customers to be found. One lady, possibly the owner behind the counter. Selections were limited very basic Chinese food and didn't look the freshest. But I was in the mood for some Chinese so we tried it anyway.

The food was acceptable at best. We have been to other HKE locations and the food was much worse quality and quantity than the others.

I normally would give it a 3 star rating, but about 2 weeks after this visit I wanted Chinese again, and rather than driving to Cypress for our favourite HKE experience at 8:30 in the evening we just went up the street to the local La Mirada HKE. When we got there we were shocked, they were closed, the hours sign on the door said they should be open til 9, but the were closed... not just closed, but gone closed, everything cleaned up, lights off, doors locked, nobody home closed. Closed and gone at 8:35ish when they are supposed to be open til 9.

Sorry LM HKE... we will not be back. We drove to the Cypress HKE, got there a little after 9 and they were still open (also list 9 as closing time) selling off the remaining food. Which to me makes sense, why throw everything away when there are people who will buy it? < Review>
I have used this gym several times whenever I traveled to San Francisco. It's a little smaller than my home gym but less crowded than other 24 Hour locations in downtown San Francisco. It has an interesting layout where treadmills are placed on the first floor facing large Windows on the street level, which makes you less bored during your exercise.

Staff are friendly and helpful in fixing my check-in problem.<//Review>

< review>
I gave this three stars because it's a pretty good facility for the city, but as far as 24 hour fitnesses go, it's below average.

First, it should really be called 18 hour fitness. I signed up for this gym with the expectation that it could accommodate my weird hours, but when I showed up to work out the first time they were closed! Keep the weekend hours in mind when signing up. (They are open 24 hours Monday through Thursday.)

The top floor has a bunch of brand new weight machines, and a variety of relatively new cable machines. The free weights are all old, but they work just the same as they always do. A lot of the cardio equipment needs a refresh. The treadmill I used kept switching speeds on me which was very frustrating. When I went to change the speed back to how I had it set, the buttons were unresponsive and I had to hop off.

The staff is super friendly, and I don't often have to wait to use equipment, especially on the weekends. If you go lunch time during the week or any time between 5pm and 8pm, good luck getting on any of the cardio equipment.

One last note: I'm hesitant to use the lockers here because I've heard of three occasions in which people's locks have been cut and their stuff stolen.<//review>

<rating>4< /rating><Text>I go weekdays around 11a-2p (somewhere in there). Never been too busy then, I always get in my bench, squats, deadlifts etc with little wait. I went at 5pm once and it was a nightmare, don't even bother (maybe that's just me).

Very clean in the locker rooms and on the equipment. Equipment rarely broken and is fixed within 2 days if it does break. Nice and sunny on the 2nd floor with a lot to look at while resting between sets. Can be a bit warm on the 2nd floor (weight area) sometimes. Reasonable amount of lockers, showers, etc. Can't speak to cardio equipment, I never use it.

2x bench press, 1 power cage w/ pullup bar, 1 squat rack,  2x incline benches, 1x decline bench, plenty of misc inclinable seats near the dumbells as well as benches without racks. Use metal plates that can be annoying to pick up. Plenty of miscellaneous machines, including a smith machine if you hate your back. Extra barbells laying around for deadlifts, etc.

This is my favorite 24hr fitness in the area, unless you need a pool, on account of the fact that it doesn't have a pool.

I've been here >6 months now.  Friendly staff.<//Text>< pictures>

My whole family comes here for their hair, nails, and waxing service.  The price is unbeatable for the quality and the service they provide. I have enjoyed Ruby's for many years. I have called in orders in the past.
I was trying their online ordering ap only to find it did not have/offer a specific item they advertise onsite, on the same page as the online order option. I didn't find this out until after I had added the several other items to my cart; I cancelled the online order and placed a call.
Still on hold over 10 mins from the time a girl put me on hold I felt I had been ignored/forgotten and tried calling on a 2nd line. It dropped into a recording about calling back and the mailbox was full.  I hung up both lines, and tried again. An Hispanic gentleman answered. I told him I'd been on hold over 10 mins and would he like to take my order. He asked if I wanted to place an order, I replied yes. Without making even an acknowledging the problem, an offer of apology, or any type discount, of he took my order. He restated my order, gave me a total, and say 7  to 10 mins to be ready.
My friend left 5 mins later estimating traffic about 5 mins. After he arrived he waited an additional 10-15 mins to get our food.
Although oddly not hot, really hardly warm, it tasted as I have had in the past.
I am sadly disappointed with this incident and will likely not try ordering from there either online or by phone again. Definately not well handled.< /Review>
